[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer report reveals a stack-based buffer overflow in the [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_json_get` function of the Mongoose codebase. While running a LibFuzzer harness [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`nesting`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in `json.c`, triggering a crash and abort.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  A stack-buffer-overflow detected by AddressSanitizer during fuzz testing. The [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow is a one-byte write beyond a fixed-size stack array.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability location  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The overflow happens in `mg_json_get` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/mongoose/src/json.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The local array [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`nesting` is declared with [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes, but the code writes at offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m under certain[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput conditions.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Call stack  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `mg_json_get` at json.[0m[1;92mc:186[0m[39m  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Observations  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The offending buffer is declared as  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     yet the logic uses another constant, `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`, for depth checks. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Overflow occurs when `depth` reaches or exceeds the intended maximum, allowing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = …` to execute out of bounds.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The original comparison used `depth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`, which fails to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguard the case `depth == MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - At line [0m[1;36m127[0m[39m of `src/json.c`, the array declaration was changed to:  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the branches handling `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m166[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m175[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks were modified from  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     to  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other changes were made to the handling of `depth` increments or to the [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer triggered an AddressSanitizer stack-buffer-overflow in the function [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_json_get` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjson.[0m[1;92mc:186[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating that the local array `nesting` was written [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout of bounds. A patch was attempted that increased the size of `nesting` from [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` to `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` and tightened the checks when [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincrementing `depth`. After applying the changes, the same overflow is still [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreported at the same stack offset, demonstrating that the patch did not eliminate [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe out-of-bounds write.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzing run invokes `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`, which calls `mg_json_get` to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnavigate a JSON buffer.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ASan reports a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write overflow on the local array `nesting`, at offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the stack frame for `mg_json_get`.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack frame shows `nesting` occupies bytes [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m62[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma length of [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut the code writes at offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m, just past the end of `nesting`.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The backtrace pins the overflow to line [0m[1;36m186[0m[39m in `json.c`, inside `mg_json_get`.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant Observations  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The variable `nesting` is declared as `unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut is used to store one element per nesting level of JSON.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The code increments `depth` whenever it sees ‘[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m’ or ‘[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m’ and then writes to [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The sanitizer indicates the write happens when `depth` equals the size of the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray, so the bounds check on `depth` is insufficient.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The value `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` differs from `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`, suggesting a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmismatch in naming or intended limit.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- At line [0m[1;36m127[0m[39m of `src/json.c`, `nesting` was changed from size `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Two conditional checks were modified:  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - For the `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` case, `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` was changed to `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m>= MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - For the `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m` case, the same comparison was tightened.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The goal was to enlarge the array by one slot and prevent writing when `depth` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreaches the limit.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Result  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer was rerun with the modified code and produced an identical [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-buffer-overflow at the same address, same frame, and same code location [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`json.[0m[1;92mc:186[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ASan reports that `nesting` still spans [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m62[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and that the write at offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains out of bounds.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The definitions and intended semantics of `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` vs. [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`. Confirm which constant governs the maximum nesting level and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere it is used elsewhere.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The logic in `mg_json_get` that [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m increments `depth`, [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m checks the depth [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlimit, and [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m writes into `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`. Verify the order of operations and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure the bounds check precedes any write.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Any other arrays or buffers in `mg_json_get` that index by `depth` or related [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariables [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., path parsing variables `ci`, `ei`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Test cases that drive extremely deep or malformed JSON input, exercising the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath-traversal logic, to understand how `depth` can exceed the buffer size.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
